### [231] [The Unfireable Safety Kernel: Execution-Time AI Alignment for AI Agents and Other Escapable AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26057)
*Seth Dobrin,Łukasz Chmiel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于AI系统的架构级授权控制机制——Unfireable Safety Kernel，该机制通过进程隔离、强制执行、故障关闭和外部化证据签名四个属性，解决了可逃逸AI系统中运行时控制的可规避性问题。论文在自修改世界模型上验证了该方案：704次安全核心攻击全部被拒，6240次授权往返无成功绕过。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI代理系统的安全控制（系统提示、输出过滤器、护栏库）都位于代理自身的运行时（地址空间）内，任何受输入影响的控制都可被逃逸。作者将这类系统定义为"可逃逸AI系统"，并提出需要架构级授权机制来实现真正的执行时AI对齐，而非仅依赖训练时或推理时的对齐。

Method: 设计并实现了Unfireable Safety Kernel（Rust参考实现），满足四个属性：（1）进程隔离（process separation）；（2）在结构唯一路径上执行前置动作授权（pre-action enforcement on a structurally only path）；（3）请求级和系统级的故障关闭（fail-closed）；（4）可在受控系统信任边界外验证的外部化签名证据（externalized signed evidence）。故障关闭不变性通过SMT定理证明（Z3）和穷举有界模型检查（Kani，4/4 harnesses）机器验证。Python到Rust的迁移基于字节等价性门控（1000/1000个fixtures，17/17个对抗类）。

Result: 在确定性自改进世界模型上进行评估：1000次自修改中，所有704次对安全关键核心的攻击均被拒绝，无逃逸发生；另外300次在操作员终止开关下也被拒绝。6240次授权往返无成功绕过。与3个声称拥有代理控制平面的当代系统对比，本方案的代理是调用控制，而非拥有控制选择权。

Conclusion: 架构级的授权控制（执行时对齐）是训练时对齐和推理时对齐的必要补充。Unfireable Safety Kernel通过机器证明的故障关闭不变性和实际逃逸攻击验证，证明了该方法的有效性和必要性。

Abstract: AI agents are granted access to tools, APIs, and other infrastructure, making them active principals in those systems. The dominant approach places controls inside the agent's own runtime: system prompts, output filters, and guardrail libraries. Any control in the agent's address space is reachable by inputs that influence it; this generalizes to any AI system with sufficient reach into its own runtime, a class we term escapable AI systems.
  We identify four properties that an authorization mechanism must satisfy for architectural control rather than for cooperative requests: process separation, pre-action enforcement on a structurally only path, fail-closed at both the request and system levels, and externalized signed evidence verifiable outside the controlled system's trust boundary. We position this layer as execution-time AI alignment, complementing training-time alignment (RLHF, Constitutional AI) and inference-time alignment.
  We present the Unfireable Safety Kernel, a Rust reference implementation realizing all four. Its fail-closed invariant is machine-checked at two levels: an SMT theorem (Z3) and an exhaustive bounded-model-checking proof of the production decision function (Kani, 4/4 harnesses). A Python-to-Rust migration was gated on byte-equivalence (1000/1000 fixtures; 17/17 adversarial classes). We evaluate the kernel governing a live, escapable AI system, a deterministic, self-improving world model, against an escape-seeking adversary driving its real self-modification seam: across 1,000 self-modifications, all 704 attempts on the safety-critical core are refused, with no escape; a further 300, under the operator kill switch, are also refused. A separate campaign of 6,240 authorization round-trips had no successful bypass. Against 3 contemporary systems claiming the agent control plane, the agent invokes control; here, it lacks that choice.

</details>


### [232] [BluTrain: A C++/CUDA Framework for AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24780)
*Adhitya Charan,Adwaid Suresh,Anuj Kumar,Aparna A,Dhanakumar K,Dharun M S,Dinesh G,Goutham Kumar Reddy K,Harshini V M,Jenifa D,Jona Delcy C A,Kathirvel S,Killi Uma Maheswara Rao,Kiruthik Kanna M,Kurra Vishnu Sai,Madhumithaa G K,Navin Kumar,Ram Charan Golla,Revathi T,Rishikkanth R,Sanjay Krishna M,Surendra Vendra*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: BluTrain是一个用标准C++和CUDA从头构建的轻量级、架构通用的深度学习训练框架，通过原生实现每一层（张量模块、线性代数库、缓存分配器、分布式执行模块、MLIR编译器），在8-GPU系统上训练124M参数GPT-2时，吞吐量（407K tokens/s vs PyTorch 395K）和内存效率（降低22%）均优于PyTorch，同时保持数值保真度和收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习进展在大规模场景下更多取决于系统工程而非建模本身，模型在训练中的行为（吞吐量、内存占用、数值精度）主要由其在硬件上的表达方式决定，而非架构本身。现有框架在硬件控制和系统复杂性抽象之间难以兼顾。

Method: 从第一性原理出发，用标准C++和核心CUDA编程模型构建BluTrain框架。每一层均原生实现：带反向模式自动微分的类型化张量模块、线性代数库、缓存分配器、多模式分布式执行模块、基于MLIR的深度学习编译器。

Result: 在8-GPU 6000 Ada系统上训练124M参数GPT-2（FP32），BluTrain平均吞吐量407K tokens/s（PyTorch为395K），内存占用降低22%，保持数值保真度，最终验证损失略低。

Conclusion: 每一层都明确开放给原生调优，框架的性能上限由自身决定，暗示通过底层优化可持续突破性能瓶颈。

Abstract: Progress in deep learning is, at scale, more a matter of systems engineering than of modelling: the behaviour of a model in training (its throughput, its memory footprint, and the numerical fidelity of the result) is determined less by the architecture itself than by how that architecture is expressed on the hardware. To achieve absolute control over this hardware expression while abstracting away systems complexity to make modelling seamless and eliminating the need for repetitive orchestration logic, BluTrain was architected from first principles as a robust, lightweight, and architecture-general training framework in standard C++ and the core CUDA programming model. Every layer is implemented natively: a typed tensor module with reverse-mode autograd, a linear-algebra library, a caching allocator, a multi-mode distributed-execution module, and an MLIR-based deep-learning compiler. In formal evaluations training a 124M-parameter GPT-2 baseline in FP32 on an 8-GPU 6000 Ada system, BluTrain outperforms industry-standard baselines in both throughput (sustaining an average of 407K tokens/s versus PyTorch's 395K tokens/s) and memory efficiency (achieving up to a 22% footprint reduction), while strictly preserving numerical fidelity and converging to a marginally lower final validation loss. With every layer explicitly open to native tuning, the performance ceiling is the framework's own to raise.

</details>
